<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d05f7291-5f7f-4d84-a1d2-a4b02ddfe26e'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>

  <span id="freeText11430219915115217627" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425504295i/13899578._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>____________________________________________<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I launched into a graceful ninja-like front roll, then stood my ground to face the monstrous heathen, fearless in my determination to vanquish the deadly foe.<br><br><br>Nah, just kidding. I bolted, discretion being the better part of not getting dead.” </i>

</blockquote><br>____________________________________________<br><br><p>
  <i>What I thought I will get from reading this:</i>
</p><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425504295ra/13899579.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>-paranormal girl who in insecure because she has lived alone all her life or has a bad family<br>-instalove in the first person she sees<br>-he will try to push her away because he is bad for her<br>-she will be saved in the end by the person she loves<br>(like every other paranormal YA nowdays)</p><br><br><p>
  <i>What I really got from reading this:</i>
</p><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298336ra/682444.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>-a great bad-ass main character who's strong and funny and one of my favorite characters of all time<br>-HILARITY(this is one of the funniest books I have ever read)<br>-solid romance<br>-a great story<br>-again hilarity(you have to read it to understand)</p><br><br>____________________________________________<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We are killers,” Matthias said.<br>Bad news.<br>“Not girls. We don’t kill girls.”<br>Good news.<br>“She’s no girl.”<br>Insulting news?<br>“What? Of course she’s a girl.”<br>“Want me to check?”<br>“Shut up, Blake,” the rest of them chorused.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>____________________________________________<br><br><a href="http://geekybookie.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">You can find the full review and more about this book on my blog!</a><br><br><p><i>Demons at Deadnight</i> is a paranormal YA who is written by some of my favorite authors of all time,and some of good friends here.It's a story worth reading.And it has everything,and I was really excited to read this because,according to the authors,I am officially a part of the Hex Boys<i>(applauding for myself*)</i>.</p><br>____________________________________________<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><br>“I reached for something to break my fall. The ground obliged.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>____________________________________________<br><br><p><i>The characters</i> are awesome.The main character is mind blowing.And believe me,this book got me laughing out loud.It is so funny,like <i>Jimmy Fallon+Ellen+Kimmel</i> funny.Seriously,you have to read it to understand:)</p><br><br>____________________________________________<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Want some ice cream?"<br>His head bumped the frame. "Ouch! What?" His voice was back to normal. He turned around. "Don't offer me ice cream. I just broke into your room and threatened you.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>____________________________________________<br><br><br><p>I highly recommend it.If you are in a good time for a solid paranormal YA,this is the best choice!</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="11430219915115217627" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1404657705" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1404657705" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1404657705?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1404657705" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10935750139354392104"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Bad things happen and somehow the Hex Boys are always nearby.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Six notorious and hextraordinarily gorgeous boys.</b><br/><b>One clumsy girl.</b><br/><b>And a horde of bloodthirsty gross demons.</b><br/>What could possibly go wrong?<br/>(well since you've asked, <b>everything</b> can go wrong.You just <b>laugh your ass off</b> while it does.)<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384624350ra/6919121.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The monstrous body heaved for a powerful flap,ready to propel us high in the air and me to my doom.It would probably strip my flesh while giving me vocabulary lessons.I'd be dead but smart</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10935750139354392104" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Bad things happen and somehow the Hex Boys are always nearby.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Six notorious and hextraordinarily gorgeous boys.</b><br><b>One clumsy girl.</b><br><b>And a horde of bloodthirsty gross demons.</b><br>What could possibly go wrong?<br>(well since you've asked, <b>everything</b> can go wrong.You just <b>laugh your ass off</b> while it does.)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384624350ra/6919121.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The monstrous body heaved for a powerful flap,ready to propel us high in the air and me to my doom.It would probably strip my flesh while giving me vocabulary lessons.I'd be dead but smarter.How's that for glass half full?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Aurora's accepted the fact that she can see demons and other supernatural creatures.But when demons start attacking her trying to kill her,she has to get help.And what's better help than 6 demon hunters with super powers who keep her secrets and constantly endanger her?<s>(that's a rhetorical question)</s><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I couldn't wrap my mind around all the weird.Demons trying to kill me,old friends re-surfacing as demon drug lords,a winged woman with cryptic messages,I glow,and now I superheal?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Why you should read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16067683.Demons_at_Deadnight__Divinicus_Nex_Chronicles___1_" title="Demons at Deadnight (Divinicus Nex Chronicles, #1) by A&amp;E Kirk" rel="nofollow noopener">Demons at Deadnight</a></u>
</b><br><br><b>Part 1 (aka the <u>mature</u> part)</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16067683.Demons_at_Deadnight__Divinicus_Nex_Chronicles___1_" title="Demons at Deadnight (Divinicus Nex Chronicles, #1) by A&amp;E Kirk" rel="nofollow noopener">Demons at Deadnight</a> is one of the books that get you hooked from the start.Yes we've heard the demon hunters story before (in fact I got some <b>Buffy the Vampire Slayer/Mortal Instruments</b> vibes and that's fine by me because I love both),but <u><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5393357.A_E_Kirk" title="A&amp;E Kirk" rel="nofollow noopener">A&amp;E Kirk</a>'s writing is fresh</u>.What took me by surpise was the extremely rich vocabulary,something that's not particularly common in urban fantasy.The writers handle masterly the words,whether it's physical descriptions or feelings or hilarious situations or battles.<br><br><b>Part 2 (aka the <u>fangirlish</u> part)</b><br><b>Holy Heck I <u>loved</u> the characters!!</b>From Aurora and her boys to her awesome family and Van Helsing the cat,everyone was a great addition to the story!And oh.my.God there were so many <b>funny scenes</b> and <b>witty retorts</b> and <b>banters</b> and sarcasm that I couldn't stop laughing!Add some <b>action scenes</b> and some sweet scenes and some <b>sizzling tension</b> between Aurora and one of the boys and that's it,you have an <b>amusing</b> and light read that may of may not have kept me up all night <s>I'm not yawning you're yawning</s><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Since when does Ayden get to save the girl?”Gigantor said.“That's my job.”<br>The Albino smirked.“Since when have you ever saved a girl?”<br>“It hasn't come up before,but clearly it would be my job.I'm the hunky one.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>How can you not love them?Blake the huge goofball,Logan the silent force,Jayden the awkward geek,Matthias the rude jerk,Tristan the cute and insecure one,and my personal favorite,<b>Ayden</b>,the arrogant smokin' one.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446195322ra/16763264.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>God he's hot.He had me grinning like a fool and dancing,until my inner voice started singing<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446195688ra/16763301.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway,if you're looking for a book to cheer you up that happens to have not one,not two,but six hot guys,<b>
  <u>READ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16067683.Demons_at_Deadnight__Divinicus_Nex_Chronicles___1_" title="Demons at Deadnight (Divinicus Nex Chronicles, #1) by A&amp;E Kirk" rel="nofollow noopener">Demons at Deadnight</a>.</u>
</b><br><br>(a special thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1402731773?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Aj's awesome review</a> that brought this book to my attention ❤)</span>
  <a data-text-id="10935750139354392104" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1402731773" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1402731773" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1402731773?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Aj the Ravenous Reader by: </span>
      Ash and Melissa (Ever So Mela)
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=easy-read">easy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=lol">lol</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=five-stars">five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=unexpectedly-good">unexpectedly-good</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1402731773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1338234821405225707"><br/>I had a really awesome weekend because of this book that gave me 404 pages of pure laughter and I’m really grateful to the awesome mother and daughter (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5393357.A_E_Kirk' title='A&E Kirk' rel='nofollow noopener'>A&E Kirk</a>) authors and to my lovely friends, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1258491314?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ash</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1042618307?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>M short for Melissa (Ever so Mela)</a> whose reviews convinced me to read the book. (Click their names for their reviews.) Actually, M kind of harassed me into reading the book and I’m ever thankful. Lol. I mean, who would not be? Six equally non-cheesy, hot heroes with equally impressive magical po</span>
  <span id="freeText1338234821405225707" style="display:none"><br>I had a really awesome weekend because of this book that gave me 404 pages of pure laughter and I’m really grateful to the awesome mother and daughter (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5393357.A_E_Kirk" title="A&amp;E Kirk" rel="nofollow noopener">A&amp;E Kirk</a>) authors and to my lovely friends, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1258491314?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Ash</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1042618307?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">M short for Melissa (Ever so Mela)</a> whose reviews convinced me to read the book. (Click their names for their reviews.) Actually, M kind of harassed me into reading the book and I’m ever thankful. Lol. I mean, who would not be? Six equally non-cheesy, hot heroes with equally impressive magical powers, (husband out of sight, I’m clear!)=<b>HYPER SWOONING SKILLS ACTIVATED! Gaaaaaaaaaah! </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443408554ra/16357377.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Imagine the younger version of these guys:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443408554i/16357378.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> *inhales, exhales (30 times) * </b><br><br>Yep! Them hotties also called the Hex boys (because they sure are hexy!) and one kick-ass, gorgeous, hilarious heroine (Aurora, why so lucky?) made me a happy gal. Lol. <br><br>The plot basically consisted of Aurora getting chased and tossed by demons, sent flying back to her home by her guardian angel, almost burned to death, hit by a car and even zapped into a state of coma and always, always ending up at the hospital. (LMAO!) And everytime it seems these Hex boys are always behind the scenes. Are they good news or bad? <b> GO READ THE BOOK!^^ </b><br><br>I know the plot isn’t to die for but it’s not every day that I end up loving all characters in a book and this is one of those extra special days because all the characters in this book (except for the demons) are to love even Bubbles (the Australian platypus pet toy of Aurora’s cute little sister.) Everyone is really funny in his/her own way that I enjoyed literally every single page of the book. <br><br>The chapters are short and easy to read and the writing is simply pleasurable. The authors’ impressive writing skills are displayed in the diverse personalities of the characters. There’s a specific language for the extremely smart hero, another for the not so smart one, a different one for Aurora’s cool parents and so on. What’s even more entertaining is the POV of the story as it is told by Aurora herself who is funny as heck. Here’s a glimpse of her colorful personality:<br><br><b> <i> “I launched into a graceful ninja-like front roll, then stood my ground to face the monstrous heathen, fearless in my determination to vanquish the deadly foe. Nah, just kidding. I bolted…” </i></b> <br><br>The last quarter of the plot was pure awesomesauce and even though the book ends with a cliffy, it’s still pure entertainment. <br><br>P.S. Thank you authors, for the bonus recipe pages. Love them! &lt;3<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1338234821405225707" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_247585502" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/247585502" />
    <a title="A." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2371160-a"><img alt="A." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405228412p2/2371160.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/247585502?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A." class="user" itemprop="url" name="A." href="/user/show/2371160-a">A.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)
          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781467984331" href="/book/show/13244372-demons-at-deadnight">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer247585502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4285812239637905564">It's our book so we're admittedly biased. But hopefully you'll enjoy it too! <br/><br/> Here's the first chapter...<br/><br/><br/>Chapter One<br/><br/>Someone’s car was totaled and it wasn’t my fault.<br/><br/>But who’s going to believe a teenager? “The demon did it” excuse, while more creative than “the dog ate my homework,” was still as unbelievable. And much more likely to get me sent to the psych ward. So when the fang-filled flying hellion barely missed me and dropped like a wrecking ball onto the SUV, exploding shattered bits of glas</span>
  <span id="freeText4285812239637905564" style="display:none">It's our book so we're admittedly biased. But hopefully you'll enjoy it too! <br /><br /> Here's the first chapter...<br /><br /><br />Chapter One<br /><br />Someone’s car was totaled and it wasn’t my fault.<br /><br />But who’s going to believe a teenager? “The demon did it” excuse, while more creative than “the dog ate my homework,” was still as unbelievable. And much more likely to get me sent to the psych ward. So when the fang-filled flying hellion barely missed me and dropped like a wrecking ball onto the SUV, exploding shattered bits of glass and vehicle parts in my direction, I ditched the scene pronto. <br /><br />And didn’t look back. The savage grunts and metallic squeals provided a hefty deterrent. Like I needed more nightmare material. <br /> <br />I shot from the trailhead’s near-empty parking lot and booked it down the road. A log-rail fence lined the thick woods, and when the demon’s furious screech closed in from behind, I cut right. One hand planted on the top rail, slick from a recent rain, I swung my legs sideways, up and over. Home free.<br /> <br />Until my bottom foot clipped the post, and I spun as if caught in a crocodile’s death roll. <br />Good news? The spongy forest floor cushioned my fall. <br /><br />Bad news? Momentum slammed my torso into a tree trunk. Couldn’t breathe. <br />But good news again. I’d rolled under a fat, bushy pine, which, along with the fading twilight, concealed my position. I heard the beast fly overhead in pursuit, taking out a few treetops on its way by. <br /><br />Yeah, that was my plan all along. Man, I’m good. Except my body. It hurt.<br /><br />My pity-party lasted until I could suck in a breath, then I pushed to my feet and headed for home. Demons salivated over remote locations like this. I needed to move. <br /> <br />Side aching, breath choppy, I shuffled-limped-jogged into town, made it to my neighborhood, and relaxed. Civilization. Where the demon wouldn’t follow and—<br /><br />Talons clicked an ominous rhythm on pavement. <br /> <br />Wrong had become my default choice. <br /><br />I ducked behind an oak, huddling, chilled in my fear-and-sweat soaked T-shirt.<br /><br />A malicious laugh churned through the air. <br /><br />“Hide and seek. My favorite. How thoughtful of you to commence a game.” A touch of crazy tinged the demon’s smooth voice. Panic twisted my heart. “Ironic, is it not, that the great Divinicus Nex cowers in fear from that which should be her fated prey? A decidedly diametric circumstance.”<br /><br />What? It’s irritating when the monster hunting you has a better vocabulary than your own. Maybe it could do my eulogy? This was crazy. I’d seen demons before but they were small, ignored me, or ran away. But this one? Well, it was a different breed. A psycho on steroids, and it wanted me dead.<br /><br />Its chances looked good. <br /><br />With my Amazonian height and auburn curls highlighted bull’s-eye-red, all I was missing was an “Eat Me” sign taped to my back.<br /><br />“You’ve got it wrong. I’m Aurora. Just some girl you don’t want kicking you back to your hellhole.” My plan to go on the offensive stemmed from my defense amounting to less than diddly and squat combined. Dusk began to devour precious daylight. My eyes ached from the frantic attempt to penetrate the emerging shadows. “Think of the embarrassment. The other demons will laugh and point, make fun of you behind your back. Your self-esteem will suffer and I’m late for dinner, so for both our sakes, I’ll let it go. Just walk away and I won’t come after you.” <br /><br />I hoped I sounded confident but I think my voice cracked. <br /><br />Diffused light flickered to life from the surrounding houses. The ornate streetlamps lining the empty streets of the quaint mountain town buzzed to life reflecting on the shimmering fog that slithered across the ground. A sporadic drizzle hummed against the leaves on the branches above.<br /><br />“I believe you suffer confusion, Nex.” The volume of its voice lowered. Had it backed off, thinking I had something up my sleeve? “I harbor no trepidation but that you remain alive. And my immutable predilection is to deliver your corpse in a profusion of pieces.” Then that laugh. <br /><br />I couldn’t comprehend much of what it said, but overall, I wasn’t getting a warm and fuzzy vibe. <br /><br />I fought a hysterical burst of laughter. I had nothing, nothing, but long legs and adrenaline. The spattering of drops above changed harmony. Feathering down through the branches, a grey mist swirled into a vague form my eyes strained to focus on. Mesmerized by its grotesque and lethal beauty, I almost waited a second too long. I ducked. With a menacing crunch, bark chunks splintered as the demon’s claws gouged into the tree where my head had been seconds before. <br /><br />I launched into a graceful ninja-like front roll, then stood my ground to face the monstrous heathen, fearless in my determination to vanquish the deadly foe. <br /><br />Nah, just kidding. I bolted, discretion being the better part of not getting dead.<br /><br />I’d been seeing demons for a few years now. Yeah, those nasty creatures that should be in hell but instead are wreaking havoc on earth. If they were close by, sometimes I could even locate them using this weird second-sight that I wished would go Helen Keller. It was the crappiest superpower on the planet, but I’d dealt with my unfortunate situation in a mature and responsible manner. I ignored it. And so did the demons.<br /><br />Until tonight when this one changed the rules and attacked while I was on my run. I’d tripped and stumbled over a rotting log which is why the SUV had taken the death blow meant for me. Wish I could say it was a deviously clever move, but the truth is I’ve got grace management issues.<br /><br />A guttural hiss vibrated the leaves. Ancient wings slapped the air with fury. The scary monster noises threatened to paralyze me, so I ignored them and concentrated on running. Fast. Counting houses to keep the panic at bay.<br /><br />Something darted out from my left, ground level. I swerved right, nearly falling, but kept going. I glanced back. A dog, one of those tiny, foo-foo things, scampered out on stubby legs, planted its feet, and started barking skyward. The demon diverted its sights from me and swooped down on the yappy mutt. <br /> <br />Dogs aren’t my thing. <br /><br />I hate dogs.<br /><br />And if this one was dumb enough to sacrifice itself for me, hallelujah. I kept running.<br /> <br />After I reversed course.<br /><br />Stupid dog. <br /><br />I dived head first and scooped up the mongrel as I slid by, feeling a rush of air from the giant beast passing overhead. A reddish sheen covered my eyes. I’d cut it so close the demon’s talon sliced through my ponytail elastic and released an onslaught of thick massive curls that cascaded over my face.<br /> <br />On foot again, I flung back my hair and continued my retreat, the squirming dog growling protests against my chest.<br /> <br />“Ungrateful mutt,” I growled back.<br /> <br />I sensed a presence looming overhead and dodged into a driveway, happy to toss the annoying pup into a garage where it tumbled under a sedan. A blow from behind lurched my body forward. I would’ve gone down but instead found myself airborne. And gaining altitude. <br /><br />Not good, because last I checked, I couldn’t fly. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4285812239637905564" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3928037385537980268">I've read this book as a birthday gift to one of my sweetest friends here in Goodreads, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1402731773?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>AJ the Ravenous Reader</a> (Click her name to read her awesome review of this book) :) <b>HAPPY BIRTHDAY, GORGEOUS!</b> <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16067683.Demons_at_Deadnight__Divinicus_Nex_Chronicles___1_' title='Demons at Deadnight (Divinicus Nex Chronicles, #1) by A&E Kirk' rel='nofollow noopener'>Demons at Deadnight</a> offered a great introduction to a series, with such an interesting premise-- featuring <i>demons</i> and <i>demon hunters</i>. This book started out really, really good. And it has tons of crazy humor that got me really cracking out loud. I love the main character <b>Aurora Lahey</b> who is all kinds of</span>
  <span id="freeText3928037385537980268" style="display:none">I've read this book as a birthday gift to one of my sweetest friends here in Goodreads, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1402731773?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">AJ the Ravenous Reader</a> (Click her name to read her awesome review of this book) :) <b>HAPPY BIRTHDAY, GORGEOUS!</b> <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16067683.Demons_at_Deadnight__Divinicus_Nex_Chronicles___1_" title="Demons at Deadnight (Divinicus Nex Chronicles, #1) by A&amp;E Kirk" rel="nofollow noopener">Demons at Deadnight</a> offered a great introduction to a series, with such an interesting premise-- featuring <i>demons</i> and <i>demon hunters</i>. This book started out really, really good. And it has tons of crazy humor that got me really cracking out loud. I love the main character <b>Aurora Lahey</b> who is all kinds of kickass. And ohmygod the boys are extremely cute and hot-- and they are 6! Not one, not two, but SIX! <b>Sign me up!</b><br><br><b>TEAM AYDEN</b> here!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415774i/820876.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What made this book a not-so-perfect book for me, however, was the writing of the authors. As an average reader and one that enjoys words that are simplistic and easy to digest, I found the writing of the authors a bit difficult to get into. There were also some descriptions that kinda made me want to repeat it all over again just to get the point. Thankfully, it was mended by the <b>humor</b> which was always present in every line. Another thing was the <b>character development</b> of the mc and the supporting ones. I love how strong they are when they're introduced during the first parts of the book, but as the story goes, most of them sort of faded out of the picture. Also, I became really exhausted with the <b>plot</b>. I was looking for a mind-blowing twist or some interesting thing that will happen but it wasn't met.<br><br>But as a whole, I have fun in this book. Aurora is such a refreshing heroine and a very different one. I admire her for being such a silly and a funny character and for being independent. While the boys always come to her rescue, she makes it a point that she's really strong enough to need them. And of course, the involvement of the family was so genuine. I love Aurora's family and their witty conversations.<br><br>Will I recommend this book? YES. It may not be a perfect YA fantasy read for me, but given the fact that it gathers strong ratings here in GR, then this might be your next favorite book. :)<br><br>Rating:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446078794i/16744105.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>

<div id="review_2043449952" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2043449952" />
    <a title="Shelly Strange" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange"><img alt="Shelly Strange" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600285315p2/25393430.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2043449952?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Strange" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Strange" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange">Shelly Strange</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-demons-devil">fantasy-demons-devil</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-urban">fantasy-urban</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-paranormal">fantasy-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=maybe-its-just-me">maybe-its-just-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2043449952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16325188250042070187">Hmmm, I am conflicted about this one. We have a MC who is a special snowflake, which is fine, but she is also annoying and TSTL. There is a combination of strength, but no wisdom or proper training, so she flings herself headlong into deadly situations constantly out of what appears to be stubbornness.<br/><br/>The Hex Boys are interesting, but there was entirely too much distrust and antagonism to find their bantering and situations enjoyable. I think Blake is my favorite, the flirt and easy-going one. I</span>
  <span id="freeText16325188250042070187" style="display:none">Hmmm, I am conflicted about this one. We have a MC who is a special snowflake, which is fine, but she is also annoying and TSTL. There is a combination of strength, but no wisdom or proper training, so she flings herself headlong into deadly situations constantly out of what appears to be stubbornness.<br /><br />The Hex Boys are interesting, but there was entirely too much distrust and antagonism to find their bantering and situations enjoyable. I think Blake is my favorite, the flirt and easy-going one. I am not sure this is true reverse-harem as she seems to have picked one guy. Maybe things change as the books progress.<br /><br />The main story is about a young girl who can see demons and meets demon hunters. They go to the same school. It reads very YA. I might give the next book a shot to see if the characters grow.<br /><br />I think my favorite character is the guardian angel. She was pretty awesome.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16325188250042070187" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_482860285" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/482860285" />
    <a title="Clarté" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6801597-clart"><img alt="Clarté" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1359200992p2/6801597.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/482860285?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Clarté" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Clarté" href="/user/show/6801597-clart">Clarté</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer482860285" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7175424641707864194"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779787.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779788.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Soooo... I effing <b>
  <i>loved</i>
</b> this book! I'm freaking happy I read it! <br/>Wut.<br/>WHAT?????<br/>You haven't read it?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779789.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>GO RIGHT NOW AND READ IT!!!</b><br/>I may throw some s bombs. No, not what you think of, you naughty, spoiler bombs. And unless you want to become a pancake under one of them and then get yourself blown up and shredded into bloody, unidentifiable pieces, you <b>LEAVE RIGHT NOW AND READ DEMONS AT DEADNIGHT!!!</b><br/><br/>For the rest of you whom I managed not to scare away, you are very welcome to read my <s>rant</s> review on </span>
  <span id="freeText7175424641707864194" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779787.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779788.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Soooo... I effing <b>
  <i>loved</i>
</b> this book! I'm freaking happy I read it! <br>Wut.<br>WHAT?????<br>You haven't read it?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779789.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>GO RIGHT NOW AND READ IT!!!</b><br>I may throw some s bombs. No, not what you think of, you naughty, spoiler bombs. And unless you want to become a pancake under one of them and then get yourself blown up and shredded into bloody, unidentifiable pieces, you <b>LEAVE RIGHT NOW AND READ DEMONS AT DEADNIGHT!!!</b><br><br>For the rest of you whom I managed not to scare away, you are very welcome to read my <s>rant</s> review on DaD. Oh, please do read it.<br><br>DaD is the story of Aurora Lahey, aka the Divinicus Nex and how she deals with her special gift, demons trying to kill her and a sextett of boys so hot, I'm pretty sure they are the reason why Earth's average temperature has risen. Now, all these wouldn't necessarily mean that DaD is such a special book (okay, maybe the six boys would... in which other book are there so many hot guys all at once?!), there are tons of books out there with the same, cliché filled idea. But not this one. And it's sneaky, because judging only by the blurb, you wouldn't think anything crazy is up, but then you have a look at the quotes from the book and...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/378969.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ta-daaa! The magic is done. Okay, at least with me, those tiny excerpts won me over and then I had no doubt that not only will I read it, but I will enjoy the hell out of it! <br><br>Boy, wasn't I right...<br><br>This book is so freaking hilarious, I can't even...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373331ra/726931.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I haven't read anything like this before. And so it was incredibly refreshing. Even more so, because despite being this funny, it could still remain serious. I know, this is confusing, I'm contradicting myself, but A&amp;E Kirk could write this novel in a way that although I was fighting not to laugh out aloud like a crazy squirrel on weed, I could still take the story seriously, feel the gravity of the situations and choices and connect with the characters. I can't thank enough for this genious writing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779790.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>About the plot. I don't really have much to say, it was good as it was. Action and sweet scenes perfectly balanced, I have no complaints.<br>But, oaaaargh the end!!! Who was that???? I hate him already, but why so hot??? I can already tell he'll cause trouble, send nasty big waves toward my ship trying to wreck it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401643ra/779791.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But no, no, <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/598513.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Though this just makes it even harder to wait for the next book. Where is the next book? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401643i/779792.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388826812i/7937118._SX540_.gif" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401644i/779794.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388826812i/7937119.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WHERE IS THE NEXT BOOK???</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401644ra/779796.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't see it anywhere. It's untitled, there's no real synopsis, and not even the <i>year</i> of the expected publication.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385263i/744126.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is just plain out cruel.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401644ra/779797.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And it hurts.<br><br>But I'm not done yet, not even close. Here come the characters!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392650ra/755882.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Aurora</u><br>I wouldn't say she's clumsy, certainly not in the I'm-so-dud-Edward-please-save-me-once-a-minute-at-least-or-I-will-accidentally-get-myself-killed-with-a-handkerchief Bella kind of way. Aurora is more likely to be extremely unlucky in that aspect, and she's totally like me. It's the kind of bad luck that always puts you in the way of a flying ball or opens the door at you face. You can't really help it, it's like you are cursed. But Rory is also an expert at knife throwing and she's not a helpless dumb protagonist. Sure, she cowers a lot, but that's just self-preservation, any normal person would run if a giant monster with extraordinary vocabulary wanted to kill them. And when it's really needed, she defeats her nightmares and steps up to save those she loves, and that's what matters. I absolutely loved being in her head, she's a genuine, strong and unique heroine.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401644ra/779798.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I'm pretty jealous of her for having such amazing friends as the Hex boys!<br><br><u>Ayden</u> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388826812ra/7937120.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh yeah, he is hot, both literally and figuratively speaking. He is the Hex boys' human torch and his job is to light girls' panties afire. Okay, it's not, but he's still making an outstanding performance in it. He is cocky and can be a jackass, got that protective bad boy thing going on, which makes me fall. He is also effing adorable when he is embarrassed and gets shy, then I'd just so love to hug him and not let go. Ever. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401644ra/779800.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401644ra/779801.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And though usually I'm not really fond of brown eyes, I could have drowned in his chocolety ones, when they glowed with that orange ember light. That's just.. wow...<br><br><u>Jayden</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388826812ra/7937121.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ayden's twin bro, our waterbender who is a genious and a total social disaster. I mean, once he starts talking, he can barely shut up and he throws fact after fact at you, no matter how embarrassing the subject is. But I love that about him, that he is so weird and he is so sweet when he is complimented, gets all red.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401644ra/779803.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Tristan</u><br>Professor Xavier, kinda, he messes with minds, so beware. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401644ra/779804.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think he doesn't really like his power, at least not after he sent Aurora to the Waiting World. Or maybe, it's just me, dunno. He is really shy, and prefers to play things safely, which is completely understandable after what happened in the past, friends getting torn up and such... <br><br><u>Logan</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401644i/779805.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The team's bowman and airbender. Though his bow and arrows are made of condensed air which is way cooler. I mean, think about it, it's light, you don't have to carry it around, just conjure it up whenever you want to, and it look totally classy, like it's made of glass. I'd so want one! He is an amazing dancer, he has wicked good taste in clothes and drives a car like he won all the races in the Fast and Furious movies.<br>He too is pretty shy, blushes a lot, and he has that innocent air around him like Tristan.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401644i/779806.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I still love him.<br><br><u>Blake</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401644i/779807.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is such a flirt! And so hilarious. No matter how dire the situation, he never misses to light up the dark scene, he always made me smile if not laugh. I love it that no matter how many times he gets snapped at, he stays cheerful and continues his dumb compliments and comments. And all the while being a perfect gentleman. I just love him so much.<br>He is in tune with the earth stuff and nature, meaning he can control pretty much everything around you, unless you are in a plastic room which I doubt.<br><br><u>Matthias</u><br>Now, he is a really hard nut to crack. He is all broody and dark, and not just because he controls darkness. There's just something about him... I think he is really wounded but he hides it with jackassery. Can't mislead me though, just makes me want to get to know him better. I have a soft spot for him, okay. And he was so sweet when Selena attacked him with her platypus and when he sewed a heart shaped patch to cover the plush's missing eye, oh my God, bring me a bucket I can melt into, I can't handle this much cuteness!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/407298.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And toward the end when he smiled and Aurora noticed and she was so shocked because she saw that Matthias has dimples.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/407299.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It just made me so happy. And he covered his mouth but still kept smiling, and I so wanted him to be real then so I could marry him. Yeah, the hard life of a fangirl...<br><br>I think that would be all. Congratulations if you read all this, and I thank you! I hope you loved/will love this book as much as I did!<br><br>In Demons at Deadnight I found a book I didn't even know I'd been looking for and had so desperately needed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7175424641707864194" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7579614526220598225">OMG! What a FUN-FREAKIN'-TASTIC book! I never expected that this is going to be so much fun that It made me giddy over the chapters,I enjoyed it so much! Thanks to my dear little sis who recommended this to me.It sure did make my day and completely awoke me from my slumps.^^<br/><br/>This is a story of a 17 year old girl,named Aurora Lahey who has recently moved back to the town she grew up in(together with her family).It's here when all the "demon-chasing Aurora" had began. Yes,our one and only female pr</span>
  <span id="freeText7579614526220598225" style="display:none">OMG! What a FUN-FREAKIN'-TASTIC book! I never expected that this is going to be so much fun that It made me giddy over the chapters,I enjoyed it so much! Thanks to my dear little sis who recommended this to me.It sure did make my day and completely awoke me from my slumps.^^<br /><br />This is a story of a 17 year old girl,named Aurora Lahey who has recently moved back to the town she grew up in(together with her family).It's here when all the "demon-chasing Aurora" had began. Yes,our one and only female protagonist here can see and track demons who were so freaking intent on finding and killer her without her knowledge why.<br /><br />But then,she met the boys..ooooh the boys! Yes,the six insanely gorgeous boys(the Hex boys)that Aurora's guardian,Gloria(I love her) advised her to stick with.But Aurora has trust issues,that's why she always end up being sent to the hospital,lol.<br /><br />Aurora's cleverness maybe a bit lame and had me constantly rolling my eyes on her goofiness,but still I loved her! This girl had me laughing from the beginning 'til the end.^^<br /><br />I loved how the authors created this book with a perfect plot,blended with a perfect humor,romance,tons of action and great characters.Not to mention the delightful images of the "hextremely hot" boys:<br />JAYDEN- the adorable care-giver<br /> BLAKE- the funny charmer<br />TRISTAN-the protective blonde<br /> LOGAN- the shy one,but fierce<br />MATTHIAS-the smart,Aussie jerk<br />And of course,there's AYDEN- the sweetest,domineering guy that I loved most.^^<br /><br />This book is my first of A&amp;E Kirk,and I'm instantly amazed by their brilliance.What a daughter-mom tandem! Can't wait to read more of your books,awesome authors!(especially the 2nd book of this series!)^^<br /><br />To those of you,who haven't read this yet..what are you still waiting for?</span>

<div id="review_1402857448" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1402857448" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1402857448?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer6532734591248734088">This book is a fast-paced fun-filled ride that had me laughing quite a bit. It's YA Urban Fantasy, and there is a very special snowflake, but it is still a burrito of awesomeness smothered in that red sauce and cheese.   <span id="freeText6532734591248734088" style="display:none">This book is a fast-paced fun-filled ride that had me laughing quite a bit. It's YA Urban Fantasy, and there is a very special snowflake, but it is still a burrito of awesomeness smothered in that red sauce and cheese. Oh, with guacamole and sour cream.... hmmm, I think I'm hungry...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456400218i/18228666.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay... I stopped for a snack for a minute. I'm back.<br>So, we have Aurora, our special snowflake. She can see demons and has spent all of her teen years running away from them. She was attacked badly, by humans, and her family moved her to their old hometown to get her away from the city. There, she meets up with her old friends from childhood - a group of guys. Sexy sexy boys, who happen to be demon hunters. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456400218i/18228667.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They are known as the "Hex Boys" around school and they don't hang out with anyone but each other, and they don't date. But, Aurora is super clumsy and special. The sexy boys save her life.<br><br>Sound familiar?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456400218i/18228668._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The great logic is that one of the sexy boys will 'pretend' to be her boyfriend so that she has a steady guard around her at all times. Of course, two of the sexy boys are fighting over this honor.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Oh. My. God," Luna blurted from Ayden's back seat. "It's a love triangle... It's just like in my book. Two guys after one girl and-"<br><br>I groaned. "That's ridiculous, Luna, this is not a love triangle."<br><br>"Says the girl in the middle of a love triangle... I've got to call Danica. Oooo," She squealed. "We could have teams. Team Ayden and Team Blake." With T-shirts and buttons and --"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456400218i/18228669.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>What a fresh idea!</i><br><br>But, here's the thing. This book is so good! The action, the wittiness, the characters are all so much fun that I never minded the special snowflake. I even liked her! I know! Crazy! I even have a strong feeling that I know where things are going with the "romance" angle, and I still don't mind. So, either I have a brain tumor, or this was just an entertaining story. Either way, I'm happy.</span>

<div id="review_263338668" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/263338668" />
    <a title="Galla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4445010-galla"><img alt="Galla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1341071385p2/4445010.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/263338668?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Galla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Galla" href="/user/show/4445010-galla">Galla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781467984331" href="/book/show/13244372-demons-at-deadnight">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4445010-galla?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4445010-galla?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer263338668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13048753250128472235">"Trust me, if I can see you, I can smite you." - Aurora Lahey<br/><br/>Holy crap, this book was fun. Okay: imagine, if you will, the Black Dagger Brotherhood, only they're teenagers, and they aren't vampires, and they don't have 400 pages each worth of angst-driven back story, and they're written with a Goonies-like combination of charm and goofiness--but instead of bikes and baby fat, they have cars and chiseled abs. Those are the Hex Boys, a crew of six demon-hunters who each have a unique supernatural </span>
  <span id="freeText13048753250128472235" style="display:none">"Trust me, if I can see you, I can smite you." - Aurora Lahey<br /><br />Holy crap, this book was fun. Okay: imagine, if you will, the Black Dagger Brotherhood, only they're teenagers, and they aren't vampires, and they don't have 400 pages each worth of angst-driven back story, and they're written with a Goonies-like combination of charm and goofiness--but instead of bikes and baby fat, they have cars and chiseled abs. Those are the Hex Boys, a crew of six demon-hunters who each have a unique supernatural ability. <br /><br />Aurora Lahey doesn't know what she is, but the demons who keep trying to kill her seem to have an idea. When her family moves back to the town they had left nearly a decade earlier, an escalating pattern of demon attacks forces her to turn to the Hex Boys for protection. Though she was childhood friends with several of them, they've changed dramatically while she was living in the big city--but then again, so has she. <br /><br />Characterization is a strong point with Aurora and the Hex Boys. Aurora is brave, loyal, funny, and devoted to her family. She can be awfully stubborn at times, but her heart is in the right place. The Hex Boys each have distinct personalities and speech patterns, ranging from humorously oafish to intensely standoffish. The banter between them and Aurora is often hilarious, even when they're fighting demonic forces of darkness. <br /><br />Unfortunately, some of those fights happen in such quick succession in the narrative--and with so little downtime in between scenes--that I'm going to make a complaint I rarely make about a novel: the pacing was too fast. At one point, I realized I had already lost track of how many times Aurora pulled off a narrow escape and found herself injured, and that was only a handful of days into the novel's timeline. A little breathing room in between action scenes would have been a welcome relief, particularly since the attack/injury/escape patterns were sometimes a little repetitive. <br /><br />That said, the concept for this novel really works, the chemistry between Aurora and her Hex Boy love interest is appealing, and the book made me laugh out loud more than once (one conversation in particular pokes fun at the proliferation of love triangles in YA literature. I snorted, for real.) </span>
  <a data-text-id="13048753250128472235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1388146776" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1388146776" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21803154-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582366251p2/21803154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1388146776?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/21803154-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone who loves demons and...romance.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=just-fine">just-fine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=great-fighting-scenes">great-fighting-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=disappointed">disappointed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=happy-ending">happy-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=ebooks-ibooks">ebooks-ibooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=deja-vu">deja-vu</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=magic">magic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1388146776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6137350189055123795"><i>
  <b>Actual rating: 3.5/5 Nex stars</b>
</i><br/><br/><u>Beginning</u><b>(3/5 stars)</b><br/><p>The story was told in Aurora Lahey's POV and it started in an intriguing way. There weren't many descriptions about settings, people, or anything special in the first few pages; instead, Aurora jumped into chaos and brought the readers with her. Best part was that she met her <s>Prince Charming</s> Hex Knight, Ayden Ishida, really soon after that. Plus, like I mentioned before, I literally choked on my own laughter from the first chapter. It was awe</p></span>
  <span id="freeText6137350189055123795" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Actual rating: 3.5/5 Nex stars</b>
</i><br /><br /><u>Beginning</u><b>(3/5 stars)</b><br /><p>The story was told in Aurora Lahey's POV and it started in an intriguing way. There weren't many descriptions about settings, people, or anything special in the first few pages; instead, Aurora jumped into chaos and brought the readers with her. Best part was that she met her <s>Prince Charming</s> Hex Knight, Ayden Ishida, really soon after that. Plus, like I mentioned before, I literally choked on my own laughter from the first chapter. It was awesomely funny!</p><br /><br /><u>Characters</u><b>(4.5/5 stars)</b><br /><p>Aurora, a seventeen-year-old, red-headed, blue-eyed girl, had some superpower that she didn't even know before those demons were chasing after her. In short, she then teamed up with the Hex Boys, 6 of them altogether and prepared to fight against the Kalifera(the most formidable demon). Of course, she wasn't ready yet; that explained why she was attacked ALL THE TIME throughout this book. Anyway, let's talk about the Hex Boys. There were <b>Ayden &amp; Jayden</b>(gorgeous twins), <b>Logan</b>(a shy albino), <b>Blake</b>(someone <s>had a huge crush on Aurora</s> who loved to play hero and dreamt about saving girls), <b>Tristan</b>(Aurora's handsome neighbor and enjoyed sneaking into her bedroom at night, lol), and <b>Matthias</b>(a stone cold, emotionless "Aussie" who only drank <s>chocolate milk</s> "Milo"). Aside from them, Aurora had a wonderful family and they played a big part in this story as well. Honestly, I love the characters more than its plot.</p><br /><br /><u>Plot</u><b>(2/5 stars)</b><br /><p>As for the plot, I personally think there was something missing all the time. At first, the sudden attack of Aurora's made me feel excited and couldn't wait to see how she got out of the mess. However, it seemed like <b>she'd always got rescued</b> by someone or something and didn't use her own fighting skills(as she claimed she had some experiences, I hope she wasn't joking about that) or her supernatural power to defeat her enemy. Maybe because I was currently biased(as you know, I just finished reading the super fast-paced, action-packed <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7896527.Throne_of_Glass__Throne_of_Glass___1_" title="Throne of Glass (Throne of Glass, #1) by Sarah J. Maas" rel="nofollow noopener">Throne of Glass</a> series), Aurora just wasn't the kind of heroine that impressed me.</p> <br /><p>Moreover, she was extremely <i>stubborn</i>! She wouldn't listen to whatever the Hex Boys told her to keep herself safe and brought more trouble for them. AND that's not what annoyed me most! Sometimes the banters between those teenage boys and Aurora were very cute, hilarious, and...brainless, but not wherever, or whenever was a good place/time for kidding. <b>The story lacked its tension and the atmosphere of anxiety</b> because of those <s>not-so-funny</s> conversations. At that time, the supposed-to-be-nervous moments turned out to be super ridiculous and childish.</p><br /><p>In my opinion, the twists in the plot were way too predictable and bland. The settings were fine. And the depictions of either the characters' movements or simple events could be more creative and vivid. It was just an ordinary story for me. Even a little bit...meh.</p><br /><br /><u>Ending</u><b>(3.5/5 stars)</b><br /><p>Although the plot was quite weak, the ending was rather interesting. It ended just a bit abruptly, leaving us a hint of cliffhanger and propelled us to read the next book. I know it sounds contradictive, but that's what I feel after reading the last part of this one. All I hope is that the story can be more action-packed and Aurora can finally control her special power at will.</p><br /><br />To sum up, I think I may still recommend this book to you despite the fact that the plot was not strong and impressive enough, but the funny characters and their humorous banters will definitely make your day. :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6137350189055123795" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer937139374" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3530373653236983963"><blockquote><b>“Her dad’s coming,” she said, voice shrill.<br/>“What?” we all said in unison.<br/>Tristan, Ayden and the fairy looked at me and said, “What?”<br/>“What?” I repeated, panicked and irritated at my lack of control in responding to a fairy I wasn’t supposed to see or hear.<br/>“What?” came their reply.<br/>“What?” I continued the theme of repetition because I lacked any form of explanation.<br/>Ayden held up a hand for silence. “Why are you ‘whatting’?”<br/>“What?”<br/>The hand again. “Okay, stop that,” Ayden said.” </b> </blockquote> <br/><br/>I can hundred-perce</span>
  <span id="freeText3530373653236983963" style="display:none"><blockquote><b>“Her dad’s coming,” she said, voice shrill.<br />“What?” we all said in unison.<br />Tristan, Ayden and the fairy looked at me and said, “What?”<br />“What?” I repeated, panicked and irritated at my lack of control in responding to a fairy I wasn’t supposed to see or hear.<br />“What?” came their reply.<br />“What?” I continued the theme of repetition because I lacked any form of explanation.<br />Ayden held up a hand for silence. “Why are you ‘whatting’?”<br />“What?”<br />The hand again. “Okay, stop that,” Ayden said.” </b> </blockquote> <br /><br />I can hundred-percent-honestly say that it's the <b>FUNNIEST</b> YA book (series) I've ever read. I'd read plenty of books I've found funny, but most of all I was laughing in my head with pokerface or just smiling. But this one always gets me laughing out loud, giggling and dying from laughter (which is really awkward when I read it in public).<br /><br /><br /><blockquote> <b> Something darted out from my left, ground level. I swerved right, nearly falling, but kept going. I glanced back. A dog, one of those tiny, foo-foo things, scampered out on stubby legs, planted its feet, and started barking skyward. The demon diverted its sights from me and swooped down on the yappy mutt.<br />Dogs aren’t my thing.<br />I hate dogs.<br />And if this one was dumb enough to sacrifice itself for me, hallelujah. I kept running.<br />After I reversed course.<br />Stupid dog. </b><br /></blockquote><br /><br />This book is freaking hilarious and it's not its only one good side. This book has amazing characters!<br /><br />The main character - <b>Aurora Lahey</b> - is one of the <i>badassest</i> badass characters I've ever met. She's funny and sarcastic, witty and clever, strong and courageous. She's so cool!<br /><br /><blockquote> <b> I launched into a graceful ninja-like front roll, then stood my ground to face the monstrous heathen, fearless in my determination to vanquish the deadly foe.<br />Nah, just kidding. I bolted, discretion being the better part of not getting dead. </b> </blockquote><br /><br />I <i>love</i> Aurora! She makes this book. And I like her relationship with her family. She loves them and she will make everything to keep them safe. <br />And her family? <b>
  <i>Jesus.</i>
</b> Her family is one of the best families I've ever read about.<br /><br />Her parents are overprotective and funny...<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“Clyde, she said it’s fine. What? Really?” Mom huffed. “Your dad wants to know if ‘fine’ is code for ‘please come home, I’m being held hostage by hormonal maniacs.’” Pause. “And if said hormonal maniacs are listening he wants them to know he will cut off vital body parts and watch them bleed out a slow and torturous death then bury said body parts on different continents throughout the world so he will never be brought to justice and will revel in their excruciating demise for the rest of his life because they had the nerve to cause his daughter any discomfort whatsoever.”<br />I grinned. “Mom, Dad didn’t say that.”<br />“I may have ad-libbed that last part. But he did ask about the hormonal maniacs.” </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />...and her siblings are hard to even describe.<br /><br /><blockquote> <b> A rap on my window. I cringed. With a smirk, Luna pushed the curtains aside.<br />She waved and opened the window.<br />“Hey, Tristan.”<br />“Hey, Luna. What’s up?”<br />“Just blackmailing my sister.”<br />“Good for you.” </b> </blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote> <b>“Mom, they could be mutant zombie serial killers by now,” Lucian warned.<br />“Enough with the mutant zombies. No more video games for you.”<br />“Fine. Can I talk about boobs?” </b> </blockquote><br /><br />You can't help but love them all.<br /><br />And now..the candy - <i>CANDIES</i> of this book. The Hex Boys. <b> SIX. GORGEOUS. HOT. DEMON HUNTER. BOYS. </b><br /><br /><blockquote> <b> “We are killers,” Matthias said.<br />Bad news.<br />“Not girls. We don’t kill girls.”<br />Good news.<br />“She’s no girl.”<br />Insulting news?<br />“What? Of course she’s a girl.”<br />“Want me to check?”<br />“Shut up, Blake,” the rest of them chorused.” </b> </blockquote><br /><br />There are:<br /><br /><u>
  <b>Kindhearted Tristan.</b>
</u><br /><br /><blockquote> <b> “Want some ice cream?”<br />His head bumped the frame. “Ouch! What?” His voice was back to normal. <br />He turned around. “Don’t offer me ice cream. I just broke into your room and<br />threatened you.” </b> </blockquote><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Shy Logan.</b>
</u><br /><br /><blockquote> <b> Logan rummaged through the cupboards. “Where’s the chocolate?<br />Girls like chocolate when they’re upset.” </b> </blockquote><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Socially awkward Jayden.</b>
</u><br /><br /><blockquote> <b>“Yes. Very good.” Jayden nodded. “But not identical. Fraternal. We developed from two distinct eggs. Identical twins develop from the splitting of one egg and—”<br />“I know,” I said. “I’ve got a pair.”<br />“Of eggs?” Jayden said.<br />Ayden closed his eyes. I would’ve needed the Heimlich maneuver if I’d been eating.<br />“No.” I shook my head. “No, I—”<br />“Because you’ve got far more than two,” Jayden said in a lecturing tone. “In<br />fact, girls are born with approximately two million eggs patiently awaiting puberty to—”<br />“Ooookay.” Ayden slung an arm around Jayden and gave him a rough squeeze. “Why don’t you leave something for Sex Ed class, huh?” </b> </blockquote><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Flirtatious Blake.</b>
</u><br /><br /><blockquote><b>“Blake, it’s not—” Ayden rubbed his eyes. “And that has nothing to do—”<br />“I could get a book,” Jayden brightened.<br />“Seduction course?” I said. “I’m sure I didn’t see that one on the high school<br />curriculum.” But it would certainly explain a few things.<br />“It’s not—” Ayden took a calming breath. “It’s one of the Mandatum’s psychology courses. The Art of Persuasion.” Ayden gritted a tight smile<br />at Blake. “And calling it anything else is what got you kicked out of the class.”</b> </blockquote><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Dark and snarky Matthias. </b>
</u><br /><br /><blockquote><b>Matthias and I exchanged disgusted looks.<br />“Over my dead body,” I said.<br />Matthias slithered a smile. “Then I’m in.”</b> </blockquote><br /><br /><u>
  <b><i>Smokin'</i> hot Aydan.</b>
</u><br /><br /><blockquote><b>“What do your parents do? Do they travel a lot"<br />My brow wrinkled. “No, they don’t.” I was tired of the interrogation. “Do yours?”<br />He blinked. “What?”<br />“Do your parents travel a lot? Are they still married? How many in your family? How old are you? What classes do you have? Boxers or briefs? What’s<br />your GPA? Do you always go around knocking strange girls off their feet and then hammering them with a barrage of personal questions?” I finished with a cocky smirk.<br />Tristan hid a grin behind his fist. Mr. Exotic leveled me a steady stare, a sly smile gaining momentum. “Do you always end up straddling the guys who do?” Tristan choked. My smile froze.<br />Crap.<br />“And as for the boxers or briefs.” One hand went to his belt buckle. “I’d be happy to…”</b> </blockquote><br /><br />It's hard to even pick favorites because in the end you'll fall for all of them. All guys are funny, cute and nice, they care a lot about Aurora and are always here to help her. There is no useless love triangle, just cool and funny friendship.<br /><br />For some people the plot might be hard to handle - sometimes it's too confusing and messy (and a little naive). I was totally okay with it though. I'm not a big fan of paranormal but I fell in love with this book.<br /><br />Overall, the book is incredible. I wholeheartedly recommend everyone to read it. If you want to die laughing - this book is for you. If you want a book about friendship - this book is for you. Go and read it if you haven't done it already!<br /><br />P.S. I want to quote entire book, so you better thank god that Goodreads has word limit.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3530373653236983963" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
