  <i>Rereading this because I've been in the reading slump from hell over the past few days, and I need to read something that I absolutely know I love....hopefully this helps me get out of this rut!</i>
</s><br/><br/><b>This book, omg I love this book! My first review still stands....except I loved it even more the 2nd time around!!! Hopefully this is exactly what I needed to get me to get invested in the books I read, at least for a while. That slu</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3473592695226333748" style="display:none"><i>I read this via Kindle Unlimited - GO CHECK IT OUT!</i><br /><br /><b>SEPTEMBER 8&amp;9 </b> -- <s>
  <i>Rereading this because I've been in the reading slump from hell over the past few days, and I need to read something that I absolutely know I love....hopefully this helps me get out of this rut!</i>
</s><br /><br /><b>This book, omg I love this book! My first review still stands....except I loved it even more the 2nd time around!!! Hopefully this is exactly what I needed to get me to get invested in the books I read, at least for a while. That slump, though it didn't last very long, lasted longer than any slump I've found myself in the last year or so.</b><br /><br />This book is just so hilarious, and so action packed. You'd think....that with SO many main characters <i>[There is Aurora, and the 6 SEXY SEXY HEXY HEX BOYS, also her family gets quite a bit of attention as well]</i> that they would all kind of blend together, but each of them have such a diverse personality, that <br />sometimes you don't even need to see the name to know who is talking. I recommend this book to...<b>Everyone</b>. Seriously! I love it <b>THAT MUCH</b>. <i>ESPECIALLY</i> the Twins, Adyen and Jayden, my favorite characters....they are so completely different, and their characters were just so nicely done....I love AYDEN! He is hot, so hot....and he isn't a total asshole, which helps. Hes just so......Hexy.....AND JAYDEN, If you need laughs, you will surely fall in love with him and all his awkward glory. Ayden may be my book boyfriend for this series, but JAYDEN is my favorite character....him and the very awesome, very furry Van Helsing. <br /><br /><i>OKAY, well I was GOING to try reading a new book...just to see if I have overcome this weird slump....sure, I can reread a book with no problems....but a new one....? WE SHALL SEE.......<b>AFTER I READ BOOK TWO</b> I can't read book one and NOT read book two....</i><br /><br /><br />--------<br /><br /><b>MAY 9&amp;10, 2015:</b> <s>I'm sorry....<b>but what the hell was up with that ending????????????</b><br /><br /><i>damn it</i><br /><br />I knew from the first <u>paragraph</u> that I was going to <b>absolutely, beyond anything, Love.This.Book!!</b>. It was so freaking hilarious, and <i>damn</i>! <b>those Hex Boys were something else</b> <br /><br />This book is definitely on the 'Favorites' list, and I really need, <b>not want</b>, <u>NEED</u> the sequel.</s><br /><br /><i>come find me:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/ReadsAsh">www.facebook.com/ReadsAsh</a><br /><b>IG:</b> ash.reads <b>Twitter:</b> @ReadsAsh</i><br /></span>

<div id="review_1493327169" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1493327169" />
    <a title="Clara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22197507-clara"><img alt="Clara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587553128p2/22197507.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1493327169?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Clara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Clara" href="/user/show/22197507-clara">Clara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22197507-clara?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22197507-clara?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22197507-clara?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1493327169" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14169821791032957720">** 2,5 stars **<br/><br/>This book started off really good, with the first scene opening with action and being <b>hilarious</b>, with a very <b>enjoyable lead character</b>. But unfortunately, the rest of the book didn’t do it for me as much as the beginning did. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>
    <i>The plot :</i>
  </u>
</b><br/>First, I thought the story was quite <b>slow</b> and that there was basically nothing much happening during the entire book. I felt like we were constantly going <b>round and round in circles</b>, me getting very frustrating at some point, even more so</span>
  <span id="freeText14169821791032957720" style="display:none">** 2,5 stars **<br /><br />This book started off really good, with the first scene opening with action and being <b>hilarious</b>, with a very <b>enjoyable lead character</b>. But unfortunately, the rest of the book didn’t do it for me as much as the beginning did. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>
    <i>The plot :</i>
  </u>
</b><br />First, I thought the story was quite <b>slow</b> and that there was basically nothing much happening during the entire book. I felt like we were constantly going <b>round and round in circles</b>, me getting very frustrating at some point, even more so because it was pretty <b>repetitive</b> : the MC, Aurora, would constantly get attacked by a demon, get hurt or knocked out (at some point I stopped counting the number of times she got knocked out) or end at the hospital, add some saving by one or two of the Hex Boys, and that’s it. It was the same <b>routine</b> over and over again for most of the book, without the story moving by an inch. <br />Also, one thing that, I’ll be honest, really got on my nerves at some point was the <b>lack of progress</b> in the <b>plot</b> and in the explanation of what the hell was going on and in the explanation of the demon world. It was so <b>frustrating</b> because both Aurora and the Hex Boys were stubborn and constantly keeping the truth form each other, basically never revealing anything concrete, which at some point became <b>ridiculous</b> because some things were so obvious that it made it look like the Hex Boys were stupid or blind for not guessing (I’m talking about Aurora hiding who she is and the Hex Boys too blind to see). This lack of any explanation led to me getting confused some times during the book, and not understanding why the MC was okay with not having any answer form the Hex Boys. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>
    <i>The characters :</i>
  </u>
</b><br />As for the <b>characters</b>, I honestly couldn’t really connect to any of them. My main issue is that they all lacked real depth and were quite <b>stereotyped</b>, especially the Hex Boys. It almost felt after a while like the authors were trying too hard to make them look like your <b>clichés</b> hot and badass guys, but unfortunately, it was not handled very well in my opinion. Also, all the characters felt too teenage sometimes a bit childish, and not mature enough. I know it’s normal for them to act like teenagers because they are teenagers, but I wish they would have been a bit more mature. <br />Regarding the relationship between Aurora and one of the Hex Boys, I was not convinced either. It was cute, sure, but it lacked some real chemistry and connection. It was <b>insta-attraction</b>, and basically Aurora was only ever raving about the guy’s looks, how hot and handsome he was, but nothing else, too bad. Also, a lot of scenes between the two were way <b>too convenient</b> in my opinion, they felt like <b>déjà vu</b> and were pretty predictable. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>
    <i>Overall :</i>
  </u>
</b><br />I really don’t like saying bad things about a book and hope it doesn’t sound mean in any way, but overall this book felt way too similar to other YA paranormal books mixed together (I kept thinking about the TMI series and the Lux series while reading this book), and unfortunately, the story and its characters <b>didn't catch my attention</b> as much as I was hoping it would. <br />But of course, the book was still quite enjoyable to read, but "ça ne cassait pas trois pattes à un canard" ! (I don't know the equivalent of this expression in English ^^)</span>
  <a data-text-id="14169821791032957720" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_572183772" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572183772" />
    <a title="Navessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa"><img alt="Navessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1444162983p2/18104163.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572183772?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Navessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Navessa" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa">Navessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=angels-demons">angels-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=lmfao">lmfao</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572183772" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15901141221589618296">Before I begin my review I have to confess that at one point while reading this book I was laughing so hard that my fiancé came into the room and told me I sounded like Stewie when he finds something to be so funny that he loses all control over what his normal laughter sounds like. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399810ra/774120.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let’s start with the main character, Aurora, aka Divinicus Nex. She’s snarky, quirky, funny and can see demons. She knows when to talk shit, when to keep her mouth shut, when to fight and when to run for the frigging</span>
  <span id="freeText15901141221589618296" style="display:none">Before I begin my review I have to confess that at one point while reading this book I was laughing so hard that my fiancé came into the room and told me I sounded like Stewie when he finds something to be so funny that he loses all control over what his normal laughter sounds like. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399810ra/774120.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let’s start with the main character, Aurora, aka Divinicus Nex. She’s snarky, quirky, funny and can see demons. She knows when to talk shit, when to keep her mouth shut, when to fight and when to run for the frigging hills. She’s tall and athletic, doesn’t have a propensity for whining and doesn’t need a man to protect her but still understands when she’s in over her head and needs to accept one’s help. Praise the literary gods! I am so frigging sick of reading about chicks with no backbone who require other people (men) to give them their ‘self-confidence’ and teach them how to not suck at life. And unlike most paranormal characters I’ve been reading about lately (<i>*sob* Why doesn’t daddy love me?</i>), she has some legitimate baggage and besides a little healthy paranoia she doesn’t let it bring her down, close her off or turn her into an emotional nut job. HOW REFRESHING. <br><br>The book starts off with Aurora being attacked by a psychotic demon that reminds me a little of my eighth grade English teacher because of his unnatural attraction to large words. She’s saved by the hero ____ (no really, you don’t get his name) and then <b> BAM </b> insta-love. No. Oh no, not again. Damn the literary gods! Why do authors keep doing this to me? Oh, wait a second. HAHAHA, it was an insta-love psych out! Yes! Praise the literary gods! You guys rock. Also, please don’t smite me for my misplaced blasphemy. Thanks.<br><br>So, no insta-love, but some serious insta-lust between her and the hero, who you eventually learn is Ayden. Add in a creepy school dripping in gargoyles, a group of raucous boys with superhuman powers, a mysterious organization, demons galore, a dash of mystery, a sprinkle of creepy and you have the perfect recipe for a great book! <br><br>Was it perfect? No. Did I find myself irritated on several occasions? Yes. Did I find myself confused when the book jumped from action to…croquet? Yes. Was it annoying that no one figured out who she was unless it was spelled out for them? Yes. I almost gave this four stars for the humor alone but I just couldn't do it. <br><br>So, good book. Could have been amazing. I’ll definitely read the next and hope the series gets better as it goes. <br><br><br><a href="http://litchickhitlist.blogspot.com/2013/04/demons-at-deadnight-by-kirk.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380236610i/681458._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="15901141221589618296" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2278937991" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2334172540923571574">Demons at Deadnight is such a fun and enjoyable read, I didn't want it to end! Teenagers fighting demons with super powers and along comes a girl who has a secret. She too has a secret, she is the one their group is looking for. She isn't sure why. They may be trying to kill her along with the demons. It is fast action and sprinkled with lots of humor. I giggled frequently! A great book with fun characters and plot, wonderful dialogue and fun fantasy.... on to book two!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

Don't worry, it's OK to dream big. :D<br/><br/>On with the review...<br/><br/><br/><b>Reasons I read this book:</b><br/><br/><b>1)</b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1033098256?book_show_action=false&page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Anna</a>: She kept gushing about it. I basically saw it, for a week straight, on my goodreads update.<br/><br/><b>2)</b><u>
  <i>The Cover</i>

  <i>The Hex boys</i>

  <span id="freeText1033490844550654803" style="display:none">A comparable description of my wedding. Meet my grooms, the <i>hex boys</i>. See how they <i>enthusiastically </i> stand in line to marry me?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411835029i/11285292._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, I know you wish you were me at this moment. Don't worry, it's OK to dream big. :D<br><br>On with the review...<br><br><br><b>Reasons I read this book:</b><br><br><b>1)</b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1033098256?book_show_action=false&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Anna</a>: She kept gushing about it. I basically saw it, for a week straight, on my goodreads update.<br><br><b>2)</b><u>
  <i>The Cover</i>
</u>: Yeah, I know. It's lead me astray sooo many times but I am nothing if not habit bound.<br><br><b>3)</b><u>
  <i>The Hex boys</i>
</u>: What? I like to have choices. <br><br><b>4)</b><u>
  <i>The authors are mother and daughter</i>
</u>: I loved that. Being in the same profession as my mom, it's just one more thing that ties us together, so seeing it here made me want to give this a try.<br><br><br>Now on with<br><b>Reasons I loved this book:</b><br><br><b>1)</b><u>
  <i>Laugh out loud humor</i>
</u>: I'm not kidding. This was me mostly throughout the entire book. The humor was quirky and realistic. The characters had me snickering and giggling which got odd looks thrown my way quite a few times.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433440ra/872242.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417704ra/826444.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>2)</b><u>
  <i>Aurora</i>
</u>: First of all I love that name( I might have a weakness for Disney). She's realistic. She's a no nonsense character with her head screwed on right. What does she do when she's in danger and way over her head? She runs like her ass is on fire. What does she do when she's prepared to win? She stands and fight. I love that she doesn't have that false sense of hero complex that most YA Female characters have nowadays but at the same time doesn't take on the damsel in distress role. It's balanced, it's <i>perfect</i>. Her inner monologue is funny as heck. She has a witty, dry sense of humor. And dear lord <i>SHE HAS A BACKBONE</i>. Can I hear a <i>Hallelujah</i>!<br><br><b>3)</b><u>
  <i>Family that cares</i>
</u>: Her family is <i>present</i>. I am so tired of reading paranormal books where the family treats the main characters like a bug beneath their feet, where they're always alone and in comes the hero to give them what they so desperately desire: <i>To be loved and wanted</i>.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390425588ra/8210581.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>NO! That was nowhere to be seen here!! The family is <i>PRESENT</i>-something I might have mentioned already- and loves her to no end. I love her family: <br>~Luna: The annoyingly-secretly fun and caring- little sister. She reads-nuff said. <br>~Lucian: The overprotecting and sometimes big mouthed little brother<br>~Selena: She's adorable. One of those five year olds that loves to talk and you can't help but listen and smile.<br>~Mom and Dad: Reminded me of my parents. Fun and dorky but overprotective and strong.<br><br><b>4)</b><u>The Hex boys<i></i></u>: Everyone was different. The fact that the authors were able to have a vast amount of main characters without them mounting up together and blurring into the same character was a <i>huge</i> relief. Again, everyone was different. Everyone had distinct personalities and quirks. You knew who said what before finishing the dialogue. <br><br><b>5)</b><u>
  <i>The writing</i>
</u>: Was fast paced, fun and compelling. It never let up and just when you thought things might die down-because <i>heloouuu</i> things can't be fun the entire 400 pages- and become monotonous <i>BAM!</i> something else happened. I was entertained constantly. <br><br><br><u>
  <i>Now, was it perfect?</i>
</u>: No. The guys were daft at times. Took them a millennium to figure out who she is. They're supposed to be smart. But that's it. I seriously cant come up with another reason for it not being perfect. <br><br><br> <br><b>
  <u>
    <i>A book I loved from beginning to end.</i>
  </u>
</b><br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30983445-anna-enchanted-by-ya" rel="nofollow noopener">Anna</a>!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402644753ra/9965876.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Thanks for the recommendation!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1033490844550654803" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_261795958" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/261795958" />
    <a title="Jen  (In the Closet With a Bibliophile)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2000351-jen-in-the-closet-with-a-bibliophile"><img alt="Jen  (In the Closet With a Bibliophile)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1341609836p2/2000351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/261795958?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen  (In the Closet With a Bibliophile)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen  (In the Closet With a Bibliophile)" href="/user/show/2000351-jen-in-the-closet-with-a-bibliophile">Jen  (In the Closet With a Bibliophile)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781467984331" href="/book/show/13244372-demons-at-deadnight">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer261795958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1584495334941288651">Seriously hilarious! This book was fabulous and suspenseful. I only wish I was lucky enough to have only guy friends in high school because WOW, that would have made things so much more pleasant. Besides, if those boys were the Hex Boys...WIN! I've a sudden urge to molest some hard rock abs. Then again, don't we all?! YUM! <br/><br/><b>Full Review (Updated 2/7/2012):</b><br/><br/>Snarky, fast and furious, Demons at Deadnight by A & E Kirk is fast paced and hilarious, providing an epically fantastic read and and seriously </span>
  <span id="freeText1584495334941288651" style="display:none">Seriously hilarious! This book was fabulous and suspenseful. I only wish I was lucky enough to have only guy friends in high school because WOW, that would have made things so much more pleasant. Besides, if those boys were the Hex Boys...WIN! I've a sudden urge to molest some hard rock abs. Then again, don't we all?! YUM! <br /><br /><b>Full Review (Updated 2/7/2012):</b><br /><br />Snarky, fast and furious, Demons at Deadnight by A &amp; E Kirk is fast paced and hilarious, providing an epically fantastic read and and seriously divine experience.<br /><br />Aurora and her family have just moved back to the town she grew up in. We aren't quite sure why they've moved back, but we know something has spurred this move, beyond the normal reasons. Aurora is welcomed into this small town with a demon shove and a totaled SUV, which is an excellent representation of the pacing of most of the story. While attempting to fight get away from this amazingly grotesque demon, Aurora bumps, and I mean literally, into the sexiness that is her neighbor and some of his friends. The Hexy Knights, six ab-tastic guys made of swoon, are Aurora's friends of old, all grown up. Together, they will run the gauntlet of demons in the hopes that Aurora will come out alive.<br /><br />Do you think you know paranormal fiction? Well, you probably do, but you don't know the amazingness of it until you've busted out Demons at Deadnight and read it from cover to cover. Aurora is fast on her feet, which is quite important due to the hordes of demons chasing after her, cause you know, they want her dead before she unleashes death upon them. Aurora, confused beyond belief how she's to deliver these killing blows, just keeps running, attempting with all her might, not to end up dead. She'd like to be alive to keep spending time with her family and lets be honest, with the Hex Boys.<br /><br />Now, I will never be able to do their personalities justice, but think 6 best friends, all boys, who's washboard abs beg for a rub and I'm sure some tongue. Beyond the hotness are the personalities. Truly witty and fun, the lot is full of the flirtatious, smoldering, brooding, thoughtful and enigmatic. Mystery swirls around their every move and action, begging...no.... PLEADING...with us to find out more about them with the hopes that maybe we can jump into the story and be apart of the Hex group. Each of them has a special power, something that they have to protect the world - beyond their muscles - from the demons at large. Together they play off each other, creating an atmosphere that rinses between intense, hilarious, heart-pounding and anger. It's an emotional Molotov cocktail I'd like thrown in my fiction more often.<br /><br />Even more than the Hex boys, Aurora is a fun protaganist. Sharp with the retorts and amazingly family oriented, she's well rounded in most areas with only one exception - emotions. As a character, I love seeing her develop and expand, but Aurora has been hurt... a lot. In Demons at Deadnight, she is snarky and pleasant, but she sometimes doesn't seem to let her emotions out except in regard to her family. I personally think this was done on purpose because as Aurora gets past the events in her life, she will realize it's okay to let herself feel. But, at times I wanted to know her deepest darkest thoughts in relation to the events happening. I think that she didn't fully allow herself to feel some of those emotions, but I have a feeling that as the series progresses, she will begin to let herself loosen up and enjoy what her life has become.<br /><br />With a host of amazing sub characters, Demons at Deadnight shows that books can contain families with thoughtful parents and siblings who you love, but drive you nuts and still be a completely excellent and realistic read. And, I just want to mention, Aurora's guardian angel Gloria. Love her.<br /><br />Overall, Demons at Deadnight was an exciting and funny read that I can't stop thinking about. The Hex boys will forever dance in my dreams and I can only hope that one day they dance off the pages and into my room. I may have to wait, but until then I give Demons at Deadnight a 4 out of 5 and recommend it to those who enjoy Young Adult Fiction with Paranormal aspects. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1584495334941288651" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11570144198226116675">I'm rating this book 4.25 stars. First of all the cover was perfect for this book. I absolutely love it. I liked this book and loved the group and family dynamic within it. The hex boys and Aurora scenes were perfectly done and the dialogue flowed naturally.   <span id="freeText11570144198226116675" style="display:none">I'm rating this book 4.25 stars. First of all the cover was perfect for this book. I absolutely love it. I liked this book and loved the group and family dynamic within it. The hex boys and Aurora scenes were perfectly done and the dialogue flowed naturally. This book had everything it needed action, fantasy, mystery, humour, and a tiny bit of romance. I'm totally team Ayden by the way. Ayden was my favourite character of this book. The heroine I liked but not loved. I was glad she wasn't stupid or that she thought she was crazy. I usually don't go with the demon fantasy category of books. Just because I don't prefer demons. That's the only reason this book wasn't five star for me. The Australian hex boy was an amazing addition to the book. And it added a little something. But overall I liked this and will definitely continue with this series. </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13740686-julia?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13740686-julia?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13740686-julia?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13740686-julia?shelf=awesome-guy">awesome-guy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13740686-julia?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13740686-julia?shelf=awesome-heroine">awesome-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13740686-julia?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1023478725" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12544680644669547347">I was pretty sure paranormal wasn't my genre before I checked my shelves and found out that, actually, 50% of my favs were paranormal. Ouch.<br/><br/>I was really excited to read <i>Demons at Deadnight</i> by A&E Kirk, 'cause words like hilarious/funny/witty were in <b>every</b> review and well, I wanted to read something hilarious/funny/witty. So I didn't read an annotation to give myself no hints about this book. And I made ​​the right decision <s>yay, finally!</s><br/><br/>Aurora Lahey's life had seemed normal (well, except for the </span>
  <span id="freeText12544680644669547347" style="display:none">I was pretty sure paranormal wasn't my genre before I checked my shelves and found out that, actually, 50% of my favs were paranormal. Ouch.<br /><br />I was really excited to read <i>Demons at Deadnight</i> by A&amp;E Kirk, 'cause words like hilarious/funny/witty were in <b>every</b> review and well, I wanted to read something hilarious/funny/witty. So I didn't read an annotation to give myself no hints about this book. And I made ​​the right decision <s>yay, finally!</s><br /><br />Aurora Lahey's life had seemed normal (well, except for the fact that she saw demons everywhere now and then) until she became a prey. And strange creatures started to call her some name which wasn't obviously hers. And until she was sitting on top of a hot guy with black hair and brown eyes. Straddling his hips. Oops.<br />And when Aurora's first day at new school ends at hospital, she isn't surprised: Hex Boys she met seem to have a lot of secrets and she intends to learn more, 'cause they don't look like who they pretend to be. And let's be honest, we all know, where all situations like this lead: if only Rora knew how much her life would change..<br /><br />First thing that made me think this book was something interesting was the fact that the MC was a redhead AND I didn't imagine her as Merida from "Brave" (no kidding, I had big problems with imagining redheads from books and was pretty shocked with this particular one). And she wasn't all that tiny-whiny girl — on the contrary — Aurora is a kick-ass witty girl, yet she's not a superheroine <s>and someone kicks her ass much more times than she does it</s>. I was dying of laughter while reading this book: <b>it IS hilarious</b>. And funny. And witty. I re-read a lot of sentences just to have a good laugh again and again.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>I launched into a graceful ninja-like front roll, then stood my ground to face the monstrous heathen, fearless in my determination to vanquish the deadly foe.<br /><br />Nah, just kidding. I bolted, discretion being the better part of not getting dead.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Don't you want to read it right now?<br /><br />The second thing I really loved was... stop. Were. The 2-7 things I loved were all these six guys. Yeah, you heard that right. Six. Guys. At first I thought it was too much. <i>"Oh, come on"</i>, — I thought — <i>"the amount of testosterone in this book is already off scale and we met just ONE guy!"</i>. But then. The Aussie. The Albino (these two are my faves). Gigantor. Tristan. Mr. Exotic. Jayden. Well, let me think again. I'M OKAY WITH THESE 6 GUYS, IT'S OKAY, NO MORE QUESTIONS ABOUT "too much", thanks. I really loved all the male characters: they're different yet they stay close to each other. And it's not like in those books where everybody falls for the MC <s>wow. It would be too much for her ego, huh? Six hot guys, gosh!</s>. My book-boyfriends-list definitely expanded.<br /><br />And the third thing was a plot. It's intriguing and while reading <i>Demons at Deadnight</i> I really wanted to know what happens next. Some moments were like "ugh, come on, guys, that's pretty obvious!", but I can't remember any bad scenes. The only thing I remember is that I was laughing a lot. Like <i>a lot</i> a lot, not just a lot. <br /><br />So if you haven't read this absolutely amazing and promising 1st book of <i>Divinicus Nex Chronicles</i>, go and read it. I promise you won't die of laughter (see, I'm writing this review, so I'm definitely alive). And if you <i>do</i>.. Well. You'd be dead but happy.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12544680644669547347" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1300750500" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5153918176212122490">* This book was so <b>hilarious</b>! And there aren't many books that can make me laugh like this one. If you want to read something light and funny - try <i>Demons at Deadnight</i>!<br/><br/><b>“Want some ice cream?"<br/>His head bumped the frame. "Ouch! What?" His voice was back to normal. He turned around. "Don't offer me ice cream. I just broke into your room and threatened you.” </b><br/><br/>*<b>The Hex Boys</b> - Ayden, Blake, Jayden, Logan, Tristan and Matthias. <br/>Every one of the characters was vastly different, which is absolutely amazing,</span>
  <span id="freeText5153918176212122490" style="display:none">* This book was so <b>hilarious</b>! And there aren't many books that can make me laugh like this one. If you want to read something light and funny - try <i>Demons at Deadnight</i>!<br><br><b>“Want some ice cream?"<br>His head bumped the frame. "Ouch! What?" His voice was back to normal. He turned around. "Don't offer me ice cream. I just broke into your room and threatened you.” </b><br><br>*<b>The Hex Boys</b> - Ayden, Blake, Jayden, Logan, Tristan and Matthias. <br>Every one of the characters was vastly different, which is absolutely amazing, especially when there is so many of them.<br><br>Those quirky, funny and protective guys won my heart entirely!<br>(This series definitely deserve more hype in my opinion. But you know what? At least I can have them all for myself!)<br><br><b>“We are killers,” Matthias said.<br>Bad news.<br>“Not girls. We don’t kill girls.”<br>Good news.<br>“She’s no girl.”<br>Insulting news?<br>“What? Of course she’s a girl.”<br>“Want me to check?”<br>“Shut up, Blake,” the rest of them chorused.” </b><br><br>* <b>Aurora </b>- Finally some realistic female protagonist. She isn't some special snowflake with perfect kickass abilities (Not that I hate them. But they are in every YA these days), but neither damsel in distress. Just ordinary girl, kind of...<br>She can see demons and have some interesting powers, which I hope will see more in the future. But she is also awkward (in a good way), funny, quirky and have trust issues, because of what happened in her past and made her family move back home. I personally loved Aurora's personality and wit.<br><br><b>“I launched into a graceful ninja-like front roll, then stood my ground to face the monstrous heathen, fearless in my determination to vanquish the deadly foe. <br><br>Nah, just kidding. I bolted, discretion being the better part of not getting dead.” </b><br><br>*Aurora's family - Her mom and dad were one of the most amazing parents I have ever read about and they were actually present and caring about the main heroine, which is really rare in YA.<br><br>Overall, If you want to read <b>hilarious, fast-paced paranormal book with believable heroine and full of adorable guys</b> - go for this one!<br><br><b>“Ironic, is it not, that the great Divinicus Nex cowers in fear from that which should be her fated prey? A decidedly diametric circumstance."<br><br>What? It's irritating when the monster hunting you has a better vocabulary than your own. Maybe it could do my eulogy?” </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404889706i/10292861.jpg" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7960881298327782811"><i>“Ironic, is it not, that the great Divinicus Nex cowers in fear from that which should be her fated prey? A decidedly diametric circumstance."<br/><br/>What? It's irritating when the monster hunting you has a better vocabulary than your own. Maybe it could do my eulogy?” </i><br/><br/><b>It's bad enough getting chased by demons. But demons with exceptional vocabularies? That just burns.</b><br/><br/>Aurora's been chased by demons, ever since her near-fatal accident. Why do they chase her? She doesn't know. All she knows is that they're</span>
  <span id="freeText7960881298327782811" style="display:none"><i>“Ironic, is it not, that the great Divinicus Nex cowers in fear from that which should be her fated prey? A decidedly diametric circumstance."<br><br>What? It's irritating when the monster hunting you has a better vocabulary than your own. Maybe it could do my eulogy?” </i><br><br><b>It's bad enough getting chased by demons. But demons with exceptional vocabularies? That just burns.</b><br><br>Aurora's been chased by demons, ever since her near-fatal accident. Why do they chase her? She doesn't know. All she knows is that they're always hot on her metaphorical tail, ugly and like to play with their food before they eat it. Food being Aurora, or the occasional stray yapping puppy. <br><br><b>Returning to a town she doesn't remember might be a nice change of scenery. Except it's not the scenery that's caught her attention.</b><br><br>It's the devilish and motley group of 'Hex Boys'. These guys are more tight-lipped than the FBI, and with more secrets to boot - plus, they come with a truckload of good looks and wit. Is it Aurora's imagination or do they know more they're letting on about the supernatural going-ons of the town? Going-ons that, until now, Aurora seems to be the only one noticing?<br><br><b>Oh, and she might light up like a Christmas tree at times. Yep - useful superpower? Check.</b><br><br>As demons threaten her family, childhood memories rise to the surface and tensions grow thick, Aurora needs to make a decision - whether to have nothing to do with the Hex Boys and to face the demons alone, or to trust in them and rely on their protection. Her life, and the life of her family, hang in the balance.<br><br><b>But are they 'Protective Hotties' or 'Charismatic Killers'?</b><br><br>Aurora doesn't know, but what she does know is that her new-found abilities need to be kept a secret. Not only from her family, but from the Hex Boys themselves...and even the one she's fallen hard for. <br><br><b>Because if Aurora turns out to be the next Divinicus Nex, there'll be more than demons hunting her down.</b><br><br><u>My thoughts</u><br><br>AMAZING!! I'm in love with a book that take you on a thrilling journey - plagued with demons, hot guys, visions and bonfires, this book will have you begging for more!!<br><br>Ayden: <br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/822/tumblrm0qsxxbdug1qia00x.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370302ra/723100.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br>I love you 'Mr Exotic'. From the moment you literally 'fell' into Aurora's life I was like "Please, please - let every chapter have him in it!!" My prayers were answered. Ayden's wit cannot be faulted and his flirtatious manner is heart-melting. And knee melting. :D<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/11/ayden.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370302ra/723101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br>Matthias:<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/692/captain.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370302ra/723102.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br>Him with his Aussie accent (even though technically we Australians don't HAVE an accent - but that's an argument for another time...!) and Milo drinking. And brooding. God, did he brood. But you have to love the over-protective types!<br><br>Blake:<br>Everytime Aurora walked into the room, he turned the charm on and was all like:<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/818/blakex.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370302ra/723103.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br>Jayden:<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/259/jayden.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">

Ev-er.<br><br>Tristan:<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/41/hislittleface.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/250149504" />
    <a title="Melissa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1922992-melissa"><img alt="Melissa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468878734p2/1922992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/250149504?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa" href="/user/show/1922992-melissa">Melissa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781467984331" href="/book/show/13244372-demons-at-deadnight">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer250149504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4762316502787579864">The book opens introducing us to the heroine, Aurora. She is described as having long auburn curly hair, blue eyes and impossibly long legs. I admit that last description made me jelly so I was looking forward to hating Aurora. But, no. In the first chapter I see that she is funny, snarky, and a bit goofy. Shoot. I was going to like her. *looks down at short legs* Oh well... ;D<br/><br/>We find that Aurora has a gift... or a curse. She can see demons and they know about her. Why? The purpose? Well, that i</span>
  <span id="freeText4762316502787579864" style="display:none">The book opens introducing us to the heroine, Aurora. She is described as having long auburn curly hair, blue eyes and impossibly long legs. I admit that last description made me jelly so I was looking forward to hating Aurora. But, no. In the first chapter I see that she is funny, snarky, and a bit goofy. Shoot. I was going to like her. *looks down at short legs* Oh well... ;D<br /><br />We find that Aurora has a gift... or a curse. She can see demons and they know about her. Why? The purpose? Well, that is part of her adventure. She has at least a couple of allies in which she can confide, but unfortunately, one is a cat and the other is an angel who she cannot get a hold of to answer even a few of her questions. She is thrown into the "protection" of the Hex Boys who have an odd reputation at her new school. Now she just has to figure out if they really want to protect her or kill her. Talk about an exhausting few weeks! This virtual non-stop action turns out to be quite a fun ride.<br /><br />Now about those Hex Boys. All of them gorgeous ('nuff said... *giggles*)! And this is how I met them in my mind: These boys are jerks! Then: These boys have a reason to be jerks, but still... To my final analysis: Oh yea, I would have totally hung out with these guys in high school. Yep, I'm a believer! There is also a possible romance going on with one of the boys, so those that insist on having your swooning in your adventure will not be disappointed. <br /><br />This book was refreshing. One main reason? No clichés I've seen around the blogoverse that annoy many of us in the YA genre. No love triangles (and one good joke about them). There is a dance around the romance, but it isn't that hair pulling out kind, but it was fun. The heroine is smart, intelligent, snarky and willing to learn. Aurora also has a family who cares about her. It feels genuine and I swear I'm going to move into that family unit. You will love the INVOLVED parents! Oh and one last cliché I personally hate with a vengeance... no cliffie! Whee! There is a thread that opens up at the end to make you want that next book, but the main adventure in this book feels complete.<br /><br />I give this book 5 stars. I just loved the fact that it proves you can have a fun book that does not have to bow to cliché. I have been wanting a book like this for a while and I can't wait to see how Aurora grows in the coming series. I also can't wait to get to know the Hex Boys even better. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4762316502787579864" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/267309844" />
    <a title="Michelle, the Bookshelf Stalker  Queen of the Undead" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3039709-michelle-the-bookshelf-stalker-queen-of-the-undead"><img alt="Michelle, the Bookshelf Stalker  Queen of the Undead" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1328667000p2/3039709.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/267309844?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2012</a>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ty/YG9Lu7L4HY5dBM86+TTROG0eLSYr+I1Enm2EwQCvjM6Xhn3GmVJ7+cjYEByPt2oddS64IGt5kFUN+LdKyig==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Oa7wIgk8FquFhhnkMqk8FjydE4ucwaxPREBuEf/9FIiVso3YRKNcQRwb/JMFYKG20lRVh7mAPG8DBAr0sx/mKQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

"That's ridiculous, Luna, this is not a love triangle."<br />"Says the girl in the middle of a love triangle. Luna ignored my protests and prattled on. "Not one Hexy Boy but two. I've got to call Danica. Oooo," she squealed and clapped her hands,"We could have teams. Team Ayden and Team Blake. With T-shirt and buttons and-"<br />"I could make a website," Lucian offered.<br />"No!" My voice pitched with panic. "No teams. No shirts. No-"<br />"I'll get you some headshots," Blake said, turning his profile towards Luna and Lucian. "I've been told the left is my best side. What do you think?"<br />"Aurora's right," Ayden said. "This is buts. Blake you can follow us-"<br />"Dude, you know no one would pick Team Ayden. You're just jealous."<br />"That's not true. My team would be way bigger than yours."<br />"Dare to dream, little man, dare to dream."<br />"Care to make a wager on it?"<br />"Absolutely."<br />"Fine. How about-"<br />"You two shut up!" I shoved myself out of the car.&rdquo;</span>
